<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бледнеть.html>бледне́ть</a> (9584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледнеть.html>бледне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blednétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побледнеть.html>побледне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pale, to fade</li>
<li>to turn white, to grow pale</li></ol>

***бледность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бледность.html>бле́дность</a> (13608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледный.html>бле́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blédnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледность.html>бле́дность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blédnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледность.html>бле́дности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледность.html>бле́дности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледность.html>бле́дностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pallor, paleness</li>
<li>insipidity, colorlessness</li></ol>

***бледный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бледный.html>бледный</a> (1701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blědьnъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blědъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бледный.html>бле́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blédnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бледне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:бледнеть.html>бледне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pale</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блеск.html>блеск</a> (2752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blěskъ</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеск.html>блеск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blesk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеск.html>бле́ска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеск.html>бле́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеск.html>бле́сков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brilliance, glitter, lustre, shine</li></ol>

***блеснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a> (5356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blьsknǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blesnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glitter, to sparkle, to flash</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be gifted with, to shine with, to sparkle with (+ instrumental)</li>
<li>to flash across one's mind <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>blesnúla</b> myslʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the thought flashed across my mind</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blestévšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<tbody><tr>

***блестеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a> (2515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blestétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glitter, to sparkle, to flash</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be gifted with, to shine with, to sparkle with (+ instrumental)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>бле́щет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>умо́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>bléščet</b> umóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not gifted with intelligence, he is not a genius</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means the same thing as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but the latter is also used figuratively. Present tense forms can coincide.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блесна.html>блесна́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blesná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестка.html>блёстка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bljóstka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блестка.html>блёстка</a> (20670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестка.html>блёстка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bljóstka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестка.html>блёстки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестка.html>блёстки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестка.html>блёсток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sparkle, sparklet</li>
<li>paillette, spangle, tinsel</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блестящий.html>блестя́щий</a> (1822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестящий.html>блестя́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blestjáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестящий.html>блестя́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blestjáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>shining, glittering, sparkling, flashing</li>
<li>brilliant</li>
<li>splendid, magnificent, fine</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blějati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bleat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰleh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bleat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***близкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близкий.html>бли́зкий</a> (594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blizъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близкий.html>бли́зкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blízkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бли́же</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ближайший.html>ближа́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close, near</li>
<li>dear, intimate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>directly concerning <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бли́же</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blíže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близ.html>близ</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bliz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вблизи.html>вблизи́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vblizí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изблизи</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izblizi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поблизости.html>побли́зости</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poblízosti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизительно.html>приблизи́тельно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priblizítelʹno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близорукий.html>близору́ко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blizorúko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поближе</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobliže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***близлежащий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близлежащий.html>близлежа́щий</a> (15239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1766. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близ.html>близ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bliz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nahegelegen</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nächstliegend</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близлежащий.html>близлежа́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blizležáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nearby, close by</li>
<li>contiguous, adjacent, neighboring</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близне́ц</a> (6786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bliznьcь</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">близна́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bliznák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">bliźniak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">blizanac</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близне́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bliznéc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близнеца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близнецы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близнецо́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близорукий.html>близору́кий</a> (13224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">близозоръкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blizozorŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with haplology.

***блин.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блин</a> (4912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mlinъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блин</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blin</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блина́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блины́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блино́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pancake (thin batter cake)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a flat round object</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computer slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> CD</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бли́нный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blínnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блинчик.html>бли́нчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blínčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блин</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blin</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">euphemistic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> exclamation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shoot! (expression of any strong emotion, euphemism for блядь!)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="редкое">редк.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="поэтическое"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a>.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:блестящий.html>блестя́щий</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> знач. 1) <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***блистать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a> (8705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blistátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glitter, to sparkle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a brilliant display, to shine, to be radiant (with), to be conspicuous (by)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молодость.html>мо́лодостью</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blistátʹ</b> krasotój i mólodostʹju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to shine (be radiant) with youth and beauty</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means the same thing as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but is also used figuratively. Present tense forms can coincide.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистающий.html>блиста́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blistájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***блиц.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блиц.html>блиц</a> (28288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Blitz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блиц.html>блиц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blic</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блиц.html>бли́ца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блиц.html>бли́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блиц.html>бли́цев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">photography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> flashlight</li>

</ol>

***блокада.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a> (5760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Blockade</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blokáda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> siege, blockade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></b> ленингра́да <a href = vnd.unilang:длиться.html>дли́лась</a> 900 <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blokáda</b> Leningráda dlílasʹ 900 dnej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the siege of Leningrad lasted 900 days</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blockade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ekonomíčeskaja <b>blokáda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">economic blockade</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> block; blocking; obstruction</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
